#################################
######## THE LONGBEARDS #########
#################################
			
### In order: 				
#		
# Line of Durin
# line of Delingur "keepers of thorin's halls"
# Line of Wegdrasil Longbeard inhabitants of Tumnogoth Iaur
# Line of Uni "merchants of the river lhun. Guardians of the river waystation of Kheledul"
# Line of Hor "Longbeard colonists of the northern blue mountains"
# Line of Gorin (Nordinbad) "Guardians of Azan-zaram"
# House Silverbeard - One time rulers of Fireheart Mine
# Line of Theklel
# Other Longbeards

##########################
### The Line of Durin ####
##########################

lineofdurin1 = { # Durin the Deathless
    name = Durin
    dynasty = dynasty_durin			
    religion = faith_khazad			
    culture = longbeards
	dna = durin_dna

    sexuality = heterosexual

    trait = education_stewardship_4

    trait = diligent 
    trait = generous
    trait = just

    trait = intellect_good_3
    trait = poet
	trait = dwarf_father

    2.2.4 = {		
        birth = yes
        give_nickname = nick_the_deathless
        effect = {
            add_character_flag = {
                flag = had_nickname_event
            }
        }	
    }			
    412.5.12 = {
        death = { death_reason = death_natural_causes }	
    }	
}
